<th class="wi_head">Work Title

</td></tr>

</th>
<td>IJG 1
</td></tr>

</th>
<td>1706
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td>French
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>à Monsieur Marchand, organiste de St-Honoré, des RR. PP. Jésuites, et du grand Convent des RR. PP. Cordeliers
